\hypertarget{_s_d_l__gfx_primitives_8c_a41cb32b84aee2742fabd5bbaced8e016}{}\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+gfx\+Primitives.\+c@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+gfx\+Primitives.\+c}!\+\_\+aaline\+Color@{\+\_\+aaline\+Color}}

\subsubsection[{\+\_\+aaline\+Color}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int \+\_\+aaline\+Color (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Surface} $\ast$}]{dst, }
\item[{{\bf Sint16}}]{x1, }
\item[{{\bf Sint16}}]{y1, }

\item[{int}]{draw\+\_\+endpoint}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{_s_d_l__gfx_primitives_8c_a41cb32b84aee2742fabd5bbaced8e016}


Internal function to draw anti-\/aliased line with alpha blending and endpoint control. 

This implementation of the Wu antialiasing code is based on Mike Abrash\textquotesingle{}s D\+D\+J article which was reprinted as Chapter 42 of his Graphics Programming Black Book, but has been optimized to work with S\+D\+L and utilizes 32-\/bit fixed-\/point arithmetic by A. Schiffler. The endpoint control allows the supression to draw the last pixel useful for rendering continous aa-\/lines with alpha$<$255.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst} & The surface to draw on. \\
\hline
{\em x1} & X coordinate of the first point of the aa-\/line. \\
\hline
{\em y1} & Y coordinate of the first point of the aa-\/line. \\
\hline
{\em x2} & X coordinate of the second point of the aa-\/line. \\
\hline
{\em y2} & Y coordinate of the second point of the aa-\/line. \\
\hline
{\em color} & The color value of the aa-\/line to draw (0x\+R\+R\+G\+G\+B\+B\+A\+A). \\
\hline
{\em draw\+\_\+endpoint} & Flag indicating if the endpoint should be drawn; draw if non-\/zero.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns 0 on success, -\/1 on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Internal pixel drawing function with alpha blending where input color in in destination format. 

Contains two alternative 32 bit alpha blending routines which can be enabled at the source level with the defines D\+E\+F\+A\+U\+L\+T\+\_\+\+A\+L\+P\+H\+A\+\_\+\+P\+I\+X\+E\+L\+\_\+\+R\+O\+U\+T\+I\+N\+E or E\+X\+P\+E\+R\+I\+M\+E\+N\+T\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+L\+P\+H\+A\+\_\+\+P\+I\+X\+E\+L\+\_\+\+R\+O\+U\+T\+I\+N\+E. Only the bits up to the surface depth are significant in the color value.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst} & The surface to draw on. \\
\hline
{\em x} & The horizontal coordinate of the pixel. \\
\hline
{\em y} & The vertical position of the pixel. \\
\hline
{\em color} & The color value of the pixel to draw. \\
\hline
{\em alpha} & The blend factor to apply while drawing.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns 0 on success, -\/1 on failure.

Arc with blending. 

Note Arc drawing is based on circle algorithm by A. Schiffler and written by D. Raber. Calculates which octants arc goes through and renders pixels accordingly.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst} & The surface to draw on. \\
\hline

\hline

\hline
{\em start} & Starting radius in degrees of the arc. 0 degrees is down, increasing counterclockwise. \\
\hline
{\em end} & Ending radius in degrees of the arc. 0 degrees is down, increasing counterclockwise. \\
\hline
{\em color} & The color value of the arc to draw (0x\+R\+R\+G\+G\+B\+B\+A\+A).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns 0 on success, -\/1 on failure.

\end{DoxyParamCaption}

Draw a character of the currently set font. 

On first call for a particular character and color combination, the function needs to generate the character surface (slower. Subsequent calls blit a cached surface (fast). Uses alpha blending if A$<$255 in color.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst} & The surface to draw on. \\
\hline
{\em x} & X (horizontal) coordinate of the upper left corner of the character. \\
\hline
{\em y} & Y (vertical) coordinate of the upper left corner of the character. \\
\hline
{\em c} & The character to draw. \\
\hline
{\em color} & The color value of the character to draw (0x\+R\+R\+G\+G\+B\+B\+A\+A).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns 0 on success, -\/1 on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Draw filled polygon with alpha blending (multi-\/threaded capable). 

Note\+: The last two parameters are optional; but are required for multithreaded operation.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst} & The surface to draw on. \\
\hline
{\em vx} & Vertex array containing X coordinates of the points of the filled polygon. \\
\hline
{\em vy} & Vertex array containing Y coordinates of the points of the filled polygon. \\
\hline
{\em n} & Number of points in the vertex array. Minimum number is 3. \\
\hline
{\em r} & The red value of the filled polygon to draw. \\
\hline
{\em g} & The green value of the filled polygon to draw. \\
\hline
{\em b} & The blue value of the filed polygon to draw. \\
\hline
{\em a} & The alpha value of the filled polygon to draw. \\
\hline
{\em poly\+Ints} & Preallocated, temporary vertex array used for sorting vertices. Required for multithreaded operation; set to N\+U\+L\+L otherwise. \\
\hline
{\em poly\+Allocated} & Flag indicating if temporary vertex array was allocated. Required for multithreaded operation; set to N\+U\+L\+L otherwise.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns 0 on success, -\/1 on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{_s_d_l__gfx_primitives_8c_afacd57651ec0e0ccab60753636862cd0}{}\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+gfx\+Primitives.\+c@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+gfx\+Primitives.\+c}!gfx\+Primitives\+Set\+Font@{gfx\+Primitives\+Set\+Font}}
\index{gfx\+Primitives\+Set\+Font@{gfx\+Primitives\+Set\+Font}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+gfx\+Primitives.\+c@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+gfx\+Primitives.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{gfx\+Primitives\+Set\+Font}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf void} gfx\+Primitives\+Set\+Font (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const {\bf void} $\ast$}]{fontdata, }
\item[{{\bf Uint32}}]{cw, }
\item[{{\bf Uint32}}]{ch}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{_s_d_l__gfx_primitives_8c_afacd57651ec0e0ccab60753636862cd0}


Sets or resets the current global font data. 

The font data array is organized in follows\+: \mbox{[}fontdata\mbox{]} = \mbox{[}character 0\mbox{]}\mbox{[}character 1\mbox{]}...\mbox{[}character 255\mbox{]} where \mbox{[}character n\mbox{]} = \mbox{[}byte 1 row 1\mbox{]}\mbox{[}byte 2 row 1\mbox{]}...\mbox{[}byte \{pitch\} row 1\mbox{]}\mbox{[}byte 1 row 2\mbox{]} ...\mbox{[}byte \{pitch\} row height\mbox{]} where \mbox{[}byte n\mbox{]} = \mbox{[}bit 0\mbox{]}...\mbox{[}bit 7\mbox{]} where \mbox{[}bit n\mbox{]} = \mbox{[}0 for transparent pixel$\vert$1 for colored pixel\mbox{]}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fontdata} & Pointer to array of font data. Set to N\+U\+L\+L, to reset global font to the default 8x8 font. \\
\hline
{\em cw} & Width of character in bytes. Ignored if fontdata==N\+U\+L\+L. \\
\hline
{\em ch} & Height of character in bytes. Ignored if fontdata==N\+U\+L\+L. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Sets current global font character rotation steps. 

Default is 0 (no rotation). 1 = 90deg clockwise. 2 = 180deg clockwise. 3 = 270deg clockwise. Changing the rotation, will reset the character cache.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em rotation} & Number of 90deg clockwise steps to rotate \\

Draws a polygon filled with the given texture. 

This standard version is calling multithreaded versions with N\+U\+L\+L cache parameters.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst} & the destination surface, \\
\hline
{\em vx} & array of x vector components \\
\hline
{\em vy} & array of x vector components \\
\hline
{\em n} & the amount of vectors in the vx and vy array \\
\hline
{\em texture} & the sdl surface to use to fill the polygon \\
\hline
{\em texture\+\_\+dx} & the offset of the texture relative to the screeen. if you move the polygon 10 pixels to the left and want the texture to apear the same you need to increase the texture\+\_\+dx value \\
\hline
{\em texture\+\_\+dy} & see texture\+\_\+dx\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns 0 on success, -\/1 on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}


Definition at line 5741 of file S\+D\+L\+\_\+gfx\+Primitives.\+c.

\hypertarget{_s_d_l__gfx_primitives_8c_a28ae354c6272da21b5753ae4ab9e1e84}{}\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+gfx\+Primitives.\+c@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+gfx\+Primitives.\+c}!textured\+Polygon\+M\+T@{textured\+Polygon\+M\+T}}
\index{textured\+Polygon\+M\+T@{textured\+Polygon\+M\+T}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+gfx\+Primitives.\+c@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+gfx\+Primitives.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{textured\+Polygon\+M\+T}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}int textured\+Polygon\+M\+T (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Surface} $\ast$}]{dst, }
\item[{const {\bf Sint16} $\ast$}]{vx, }
\item[{const {\bf Sint16} $\ast$}]{vy, }
\item[{int}]{n, }
\item[{{\bf S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Surface} $\ast$}]{texture, }
\item[{int}]{texture\+\_\+dx, }
\item[{int}]{texture\+\_\+dy, }
\item[{int $\ast$$\ast$}]{poly\+Ints, }
\item[{int $\ast$}]{poly\+Allocated}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{_s_d_l__gfx_primitives_8c_a28ae354c6272da21b5753ae4ab9e1e84}


Draws a polygon filled with the given texture (Multi-\/\+Threading Capable). 

This operation use internally S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Blit\+Surface for lines of the source texture. It supports alpha drawing.

To get the best performance of this operation you need to make sure the texture and the dst surface have the same format (see \href{http://docs.mandragor.org/files/Common_libs_documentation/SDL/SDL_Documentation_project_en/sdlblitsurface.html}{\tt http\+://docs.\+mandragor.\+org/files/\+Common\+\_\+libs\+\_\+documentation/\+S\+D\+L/\+S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Documentation\+\_\+project\+\_\+en/sdlblitsurface.\+html}). The last two parameters are optional, but required for multithreaded operation. When set to N\+U\+L\+L, uses global static temp array.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst} & the destination surface, \\
\hline
{\em vx} & array of x vector components \\
\hline
{\em vy} & array of x vector components \\
\hline
{\em n} & the amount of vectors in the vx and vy array \\
\hline
{\em texture} & the sdl surface to use to fill the polygon \\
\hline
{\em texture\+\_\+dx} & the offset of the texture relative to the screeen. if you move the polygon 10 pixels to the left and want the texture to apear the same you need to increase the texture\+\_\+dx value \\
\hline
{\em texture\+\_\+dy} & see texture\+\_\+dx \\
\hline
{\em poly\+Ints} & preallocated temp array storage for vertex sorting (used for multi-\/threaded operation) \\
\hline
{\em poly\+Allocated} & flag indicating oif the temp array was allocated (used for multi-\/threaded operation)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns 0 on success, -\/1 on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
